./RETURN_FILES/DISCOVER/DNLOAD/discover_DISPIMGE_file_dnload.exp:spawn ftp $destination_box
./RETURN_FILES/DISCOVER/DNLOAD/discover_DISPIMGE_file_dnload.exp:    "\n230*ftp>"  {set rightnow [clock seconds]
./RETURN_FILES/DISCOVER/DNLOAD/discover_DISPIMGE_file_dnload.exp:    "*ftp>"                  {send "bye\r"}
./RETURN_FILES/DISCOVER/DNLOAD/discover_DISPIMGE_file_dnload.exp:    "\n530*Login failed.*ftp>"     {send_user "failed login\n"; bailout "Failed login during Discover file upload" 1}
